. //Step 2 Creates banners.  This process is lengthy.  Be sure to disable any
>  programs that can cause write conflicts, ie dropbox.
. //Replace any old version of the banner file with the same name
. use "Input Data Files/BannersCleanser.dta", clear

. export excel test using "Outputs/tabulations `c(current_date)'.xlsx", sheet

. foreach qvar in `qvars'{
  2.                                                         local row = 5
  3.                                                         set matsize 1000
> 0
  4.                                                         //Load Data
.                                                         use "Outputs/Step4.
> dta", clear
  5.                                                 
.                                                 // generate variables for w
> hich act as the metrics.  Those variables that need summed
.                                                 gen float dummy_total = 1
  6.                                                 gen float  weighted_tota
> l = TT_Survey_Weight
  7.                                                 gen float sum_dummy_tota
> l = dummy_total
  8.                                                 gen float sum_weighted_t
> otal  = weighted_total
  9. 
.                                                 // create a new column for 
> each of the values within those variables
.                                                 foreach cvar in `cvars'{
 10.                                                                         
>                         levelsof `cvar', local(levels) 
 11.                                                                         
>                         foreach l of local levels {             
 12.                                                                         
>                                                                            
>              local smallvar = substr("`cvar'",strlen("`cvar'")-strpos(strre
> verse("`cvar'"), "_")+2,.)
 13.                                                                         
>                                                                            
>              local g_`smallvar'_`l' : variable label `cvar'
 14.                                                                         
>                                                                            
>              //local g_`smallvar'_`l'_val : variable `cvar' `l'
.                                                                            
>                                                                            
>           gen g_`smallvar'_`l' = .
 15.                                                                         
>                                                                            
>              replace g_`smallvar'_`l' = sum_weighted_total if `cvar' == `l'
 16.                                                                         
>                                                                            
>              local smallval_lab : label `smallvar' `l'
 17.                                                                         
>                                                                            
>              label variable g_`smallvar'_`l' "`smallvar' = smallval_lab"   
>                                                                            
>                                                                        
 18.                                                                         
>                                                                            
>              }
 19.                                                                         
>                         }
 20. 
.                                                 //create new dataset only w
> ith summed values of those variables that have been identified as having th
> eir own sheets
.                                                 collapse (sum) sum_weighted
> _total sum_dummy_total g_* , by(`qvar')
 21.                                                 
.         
.                                                 // create subtotals
.                                                 egen sub_dummy_total     = 
> total(sum_dummy_total)
 22.                                                 egen sub_weighted_total 
>  = total(sum_weighted_total)
 23.                                                 
.                                                 //calculate the percentage 
> of the subtotal for any of the columns created above
.                                                 local gs g*
 24.                                                 foreach avar of varlist 
> `gs' {
 25.                                                                         
>                         egen sub_`avar' = total(`avar')
 26.                                                                         
>                         gen per_`avar' = `avar'/sub_`avar'
 27.                                                                         
>                         
.                                                                            
>                      local ques_start= substr("`avar'",3,.)
 28.                                                                         
>                         local splitat = strpos("`ques_start'","_")
 29.                                                                         
>                         local ques_word= substr("`ques_start'",1,`splitat'-
> 1)
 30.                                                                         
>                         local ques_num= substr("`ques_start'",`splitat'+1,.
> )
 31.                                                                         
>                         local ques_lab : label `ques_word' `ques_num'
 32.                                                                         
>                         
.                                                                            
>                      label variable per_`avar' "`ques_word' = `ques_lab'"
 33.                                                                         
>                         }
 34.                                                 
.                                                 //create outputs        
.                                                 gen per_wght_total  = sum_w
> eighted_total / sub_weighted_total
 35.                                                 label variable per_wght_
> total "% Total Sample, Weighted"
 36.                                                 gen per_dummy_total  = s
> um_dummy_total / sub_dummy_total
 37.                                                 label variable per_dummy
> _total "% Total Sample, Unweighted"
 38.                                                 label variable sum_weigh
> ted_total "# Total Sample, Weighted"
 39.                                                 label variable sum_dummy
> _total "# Total Sample, Unweighted"     
 40. 
.                                                         //created a matrix 
> of the results so that the results can be outputeed via putexcel command
.                                                         //mkmat `qvar' sum_
> dummy_total per_dummy_total sum_weighted_total per_wght_total  per_g*
.                                                 
.                                                         //calculates the te
> st for difference in population proportions
.                                                                 foreach ava
> r of varlist `gs' {
 41.                                                                 //Numera
> tor
.                                                                 gen num_`av
> ar'= per_`avar' - per_wght_total
 42.                                                                 //Pooled
>  sample proportion.
.                                                                 gen psp_`av
> ar' = (`avar' + sum_weighted_total)/(sub_`avar' + sub_weighted_total)
 43.                                                                 //Standa
> rd Error
.                                                                 gen SE_`ava
> r' = sqrt(((1-psp_`avar')*psp_`avar')*(1/sub_weighted_total + 1/sub_`avar')
> )
 44.                                                                 //Z-Scor
> e
.                                                                 gen z_`avar
> ' = abs(num_`avar' / SE_`avar')
 45.                                                                 // P-Val
> ue
.                                                                 gen p_`avar
> ' = 2*(1-normal(abs(z_`avar'))) 
 46.                                                                 //make m
> atrix
.                                                                 mkmat p_`av
> ar'
 47.                                                                 //add co
> lors
.                                                                 gen str col
> or_`avar' = "white"
 48.                                                                 replace 
> color_`avar' = "lightblue" if p_`avar'<=.05 & num_`avar'>0
 49.                                                                 replace 
> color_`avar' = "lightsalmon" if p_`avar'<=.05 & num_`avar'<0
 50.                                                                 
.                                                                 //Create la
> bels
.                                                                 local ques_
> start= substr("`avar'",3,.)
 51.                                                                 local sp
> litat = strpos("`ques_start'","_")
 52.                                                                 local qu
> es_word= substr("`ques_start'",1,`splitat'-1)
 53.                                                                 local qu
> es_num= substr("`ques_start'",`splitat'+1,.)
 54.                                                                 local qu
> es_lab : label `ques_word' `ques_num'
 55.                                                                 
.                                                                 label varia
> ble p_`avar' "P-val `ques_word' = `ques_lab'"
 56.                                                                 
.                                                                 }       
 57.

> ts
